# telegram_webhook.py
from flask import Flask, request
from Companion_Engine.logic_handler import parse_command
app = Flask(__name__)
def webhook():
data = request.json
msg = data.get("message", {}).get("text", "")
reply = parse_command(msg)
return {"text": reply}, 200

from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse

@app.post("/reflex")
async def reflex_endpoint(request: Request):

message = data.get("message", "")
# ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ (‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏π‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì)

from fastapi import FastAPI, Request
from pydantic import BaseModel
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
app = FastAPI()
class Message(BaseModel):
message: str
@app.post("/reflex")
async def reflex_response(msg: Message):
response_text = f"‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏π‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞: {msg.message} üñ§"
return JSONResponse(content={"reply": response_text})
